
    [TestMethod]
    public async Task player_name()
    {
        await Load_GB_PokemonRed(6);

        var mapper = await GameHookClient.GetMapperAsync();
    
        mapper.AssertAreEqual("player.name", 0xD158, [128, 128, 128, 128, 128, 128, 128, 80, 0, 0, 0], "AAAAAAA");
    }
